<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступать.html>ступа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stupátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:остыть.html>осты́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ostýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-вать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">осты́нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ostýnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***осуждение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осуждение.html>осужде́ние</a> (10031)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осуждение.html>осужде́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osuždénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осуждение.html>осужде́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осуждение.html>осужде́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осуждение.html>осужде́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>conviction <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">judgement of guilt</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>animadversion, condemnation <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">criticism, a critical remark</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***осунуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осунуться.html>осу́нуться</a> (11910)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сунуть.html>су́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">súnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осунуться.html>осу́нуться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osúnutʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to get/grow/look pinched, to become thin and hollow-cheeked, to look drawn/haggard, to become peaky
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:осунуться.html>осу́нулся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>osúnulsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has a pinched face; his cheeks are sunken</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>

***осушить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осушить.html>осуши́ть</a> (18533)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушить.html>суши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sušítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осушить.html>осуши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osušítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">осуша́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dry, to drain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осушить.html>осуши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́то</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osušítʹ</b> bolóto</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drain/reclaim a marsh</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осушить.html>осуши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слёзы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osušítʹ</b> sljózy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dry one's tears</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drain, to drink up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осушить.html>осуши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стакан.html>стака́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osušítʹ</b> stakán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drain one's glass</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***осуществить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осуществить.html>осуществи́ть</a> (4792)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:существо.html>существо́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">suščestvó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осуществить.html>осуществи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osuščestvítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осуществлять.html>осуществля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to realize, to accomplish, to fulfill, to put into practice</li>

***осуществлённый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осуществлённый.html>осуществлённый</a> (4792)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осуществлявшийся.html>осуществля́вшийся</a> (5570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***осуществляться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осуществляться.html>осуществля́ться</a> (5570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осуществлять.html>осуществля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osuščestvljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осуществляться.html>осуществля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osuščestvljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осуществиться.html>осуществи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be carried out; to be realized; to come true; to come to be; to be put into effect</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осуществлять.html>осуществля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osuščestvljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***осчастливить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осчастливить.html>осчастли́вить</a> (15309)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:счастливый.html>счастли́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sčastlívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or less likely <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">счастли́вить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sčastlívitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осчастливить.html>осчастли́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osčastlívitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">осчастли́вливать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make happy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:счастливый.html>счастли́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sčastlívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:счастливый.html>счастли́во</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sčastlívo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***осыпать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осыпа́ть</a> (9795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осы́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osýpatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осыпа́ть</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to strew <i>(with)</i>, to shower <i>(on)</i></li>
<li>to shower <i>(with)</i>, to heap <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осы́пать</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:подарок.html>пода́рками</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:почесть.html>по́честями</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osýpatʹ</b> kovó-libo podárkami (póčestjami)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shower someone with gifts (honours)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осы́пать</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́рами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osýpatʹ</b> kovó-libo udárami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shower/rain blows upon someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осы́пать</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:насмешка.html>насме́шками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osýpatʹ</b> kovó-libo nasméškami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to heap ridicule on someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осы́пать</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:брань.html>бра́нью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osýpatʹ</b> kovó-libo bránʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to heap abuse on someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осы́пать</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:упрек.html>упрёками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osýpatʹ</b> kovó-libo uprjókami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hurl reproaches at someone</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(leaves, petals)</i> to shed</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осы́пать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осыпа́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:насмешка.html>насме́шками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osypátʹ</b> kovó-libo nasméškami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to heap ridicule on someone</span></div></dd>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осы́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпаться.html>осы́паться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osýpatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпаться.html>осыпа́ться</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to crumble</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">flowers, leaves</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to fall <i>(off)</i>, <i>(crops)</i> to shed its grain</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осы́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осыпь</a> (14799)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>о́сыпь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ósypʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпь.html>о́сыпи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпь.html>о́сыпи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпь.html>о́сыпей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>scree, talus</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осыпа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osypatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осы́пь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osýpʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">second-person singular imperative perfective of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осыпать.html>осы́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***ось.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ось.html>ось</a> (4429)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:ось.html>ось</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*osь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">axle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>In the sense of "operating system", is an adaptation of the English acronym <span class="Latn" lang="en">OS</span> in the same sense.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ось.html>ось</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ось.html>о́си</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ось.html>о́си</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ось.html>осе́й</a></b>)
</p>

<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1967</b>,  “Song about Bears”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:кавказский.html>кавка́зская</a> <a href = Caucasian Style</a></cite> |  | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.karaoke.ru/artists/film-kavkazskaja-plennica/text/pesenka-o-medvedyakh/">[1]</a></sup> (film):</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">где́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мороз.html>моро́з</a>, / <a href = vnd.unilang:тереться.html>тру́тся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спино́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:медведь.html>медве́ди</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:плыть.html>плыву́т</a> столе́тья, / <a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спя́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подо.html>подо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лед.html>льдо́м</a> <a href = Latn">Gdé-to na bélom svéte, / Tám, gde vsegdá moróz, / Trútsja spinój medvédi / O zemnúju <b>ósʹ</b>. / Mímo plyvút stolétʹja, / Spját podo lʹdóm morjá, / Trútsja ob <b>ósʹ</b> medvédi, / Vértitsja zemljá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Somewhere in the world, / Where it is always cold, / Bears are rubbing their backs, / Against the earth's <b>axis</b>. / The centuries are swimming by, <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осьминог.html>осьмино́г</a> (16249)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">осмь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osmĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (Modern Russian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восемь.html>во́семь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vósemʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*osmь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive plural of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*noga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">foot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
